					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = naval_effort_built
					}
					any_owned_state = {
						dockyard > 0
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						dockyard > 0
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
			}
		}
	}

						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = naval_effort_built
					}
					any_owned_state = {
						dockyard > 0
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						dockyard > 0
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
			}
		}
	}
